YES

********************************************************************************
Proof Outline:

Remains to prove termination of a 3-rules system (3 strict rules).
Reversing the system.
Remains to prove termination of a 3-rules system (3 strict rules).
Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
Remains to prove termination of a 7-rules system (4 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 88-rules system (16 strict rules).
Removing 5 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 83-rules system (16 strict rules).
Removing 8 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 75-rules system (14 strict rules).
Removing 6 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 69-rules system (10 strict rules).
Applying sparse tiling TROC(2) [Geser/Hofbauer/Waldmann, FSCD 2019].
Remains to prove termination of a 995-rules system (40 strict rules).
Removing 95 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 900-rules system (40 strict rules).
Removing 79 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 821-rules system (33 strict rules).
Removing 26 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 795-rules system (31 strict rules).
Removing 377 rules by a matrix interpretation of dimension 2 [Hofbauer/Waldmann, RTA 2006].
Remains to prove termination of a 418-rules system (0 strict rules).
QED

Proof:

After renaming modulo the bijection { a ↦ 0, b ↦ 1, c ↦ 2 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 3-rules system (3 strict rules)
{ 0 ⟶ ,
  0 0 ⟶ 0 1 2 1 0 ,
  1 2 ⟶ 2 0 }

Reversing the system.
After renaming modulo the bijection { 0 ↦ 0, 1 ↦ 1, 2 ↦ 2 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 3-rules system (3 strict rules)
{ 0 ⟶ ,
  0 0 ⟶ 0 1 2 1 0 ,
  2 1 ⟶ 0 2 }

Applying the dependency pairs transformation [Arts, CAAP 1996], [Arts/Giesl, RTA 1996].
  Here, ↑ marks so-called defined symbols.
After renaming modulo the bijection { (0,↑) ↦ 0, (0,↓) ↦ 1, (1,↓) ↦ 2, (2,↓) ↦ 3, (2,↑) ↦ 4 },
  it remains to prove termination of the 7-rules system (4 strict rules)
{ 0 1 ⟶ 0 2 3 2 1 ,
  0 1 ⟶ 4 2 1 ,
  4 2 ⟶ 0 3 ,
  4 2 ⟶ 4 ,
  1 →= ,
  1 1 →= 1 2 3 2 1 ,
  3 2 →= 1 3 }
